									<div class="field-label">Description</div>
			<div class="job_description widget"><p><strong>** Apply at this&nbsp;<a href="https://putnam.referrals.selectminds.com/college/jobs/business-process-management-and-automation-developer-359" target="_blank">link</a> instead of in Nuworks **</strong></p>
<p><br><br></p>
<p><strong>Position Description:</strong>&nbsp;<br><br>The BPM &amp; Automation Developer Co-op role is an opportunity for a business or computer science student to work with the latest platforms in support of Intelligent Automation and Business Process Management with an agile team of analysts and developers. You will be working within a scrum team to help redesign and automate processes across Putnam's operations, using Appian (low-code BPM platform) and UiPath (Robotic Process Automation platform). This will include exposure to process mapping, UI/UX, scripting, database design and programming, as well as web services.<br><br>&nbsp;<br><br><strong>Responsibilities:</strong><br><br><br></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Document and analyze current business processes and identify opportunities for improvement through re-engineering or automation</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Implement new processes, process changes, and automations using Appian, UiPath and other platforms</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Integrate various systems together using RESTful web services and managed solutions from Amazon Web Services and Azure such as optical character recognition</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Perform thorough testing of new processes and changes, as well as test and validate patches and upgrades to core platforms</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p><br><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br><br><strong>Education Requirements:</strong><br><br><br></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>2 years into a Computer Science, Business Administration, or Information Systems degree or related discipline</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p><br><br>&nbsp;<br><br><strong>Desirable Qualifications:</strong><br><br><br></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>You must have a reasonable level of proficiency in a procedural language such as Java, C, C++, Visual Basic, or Python</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Exposure to (or knowledge of) Relational Databases, SQL, Web Services, Windows desktop environment</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Prior experience automating desktop applications (through macros or other) is highly desired</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Ability to quickly learn/adapt to new platforms and programming languages as appropriate</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Ability to work in a fast paced environment, independently and as part of a team</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p></p>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>Must be self-motivated, have strong ability to multitask, and be attentive to detail.</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p><br><br>&nbsp;<br><br><strong>Work Schedule: </strong>Monday - Friday 9:00 a.m. to 5:00 p.m.<br><br>&nbsp;<br><br><strong>About Putnam Investments:</strong><br><br>Since 1937, when George Putnam created a prudent mix of stocks and bonds in a single, professionally managed portfolio, we have championed the wisdom of the balanced approach. Today, we offer investors a world of equity, fixed-income, multi-asset, and absolute return portfolios so investors can pursue a range of financial goals. Our seasoned portfolio managers seek superior results over time, backed by original, fundamental research on a global scale. We believe in service excellence, in the value of experienced financial advice, and in putting clients first in everything we do.<br><br>&nbsp;<br><br>At Putnam we are&nbsp;committed&nbsp;to a diverse&nbsp;workforce&nbsp;and take&nbsp;positive&nbsp;steps to ensure&nbsp;equal opportunity&nbsp;in our recruitment process. We also undertake to hire, develop and retain the most talented individuals by valuing the varied skills that you bring because we believe diversity fosters creativity and innovation.<br><br>&nbsp;<br><br><strong>Candidates must be a U.S. citizen or national, refugee, asylee, or lawful permanent resident</strong><br><br><br>&nbsp;</p></div>

var custom_close_onclick = 'disableResumeButtons(false)'; 
function addNewDocumentToForm(formname,newdocclass,updatefield,fileid,label) { 
  multisel = false; 
  parent_form = document.getElementById(formname); 
  temp_field = parent_form.elements['dnf_class_values['+newdocclass+']['+updatefield+']']; 
  parent_field = document.getElementById(temp_field.id); 
  if(typeof(parent_field)=='undefined') { 
    parent_field = parent_form.elements['dnf_class_values_'+newdocclass+'__'+updatefield+'_']; 
    multisel = true; 
  } 
  addNewOption(parent_field,fileid,label); 
  if(multisel) { 
    parent_field.onchange(); 
  } 
} 
function addNewOption(select,option_value,option_name) { 
  var option = document.createElement('option'); 
  var option_text = document.createTextNode(option_name); 
  option.value = option_value; 
  option.name = option_name; 
  option.selected = true; 
  option.appendChild(option_text); 
  select.appendChild(option); 
} 
</script>

function printPreview(warn) {
    var confirmation = true;
    if (warn == true) {
        confirmation = confirm('Only saved data will be printed. Click OK to continue or Cancel to go back and save first.');
    }
    if (confirmation) {
        window.open('/students/index.php?_do_print=1&print_v=1604536208','printer_friendly','location=0,menubar=1,toolbar=1,resizable=1,scrollbars=1');
    } else {
        return false;
    }
}

var shouldprint = false;

function printQuick() {
    frame = frames['__hiddenframe'+nextFrame()];
    frame.location.href = '/students/index.php?_do_print=1&_do_print_quick=1&version=1604536208';
    shouldprint = true;
}

function printMeOnce(frame) {
    if (shouldprint) {
        frame.focus();
        if (typeof(frame.window.print) == 'function') {
            frame.window.print();
        } else {
            print();
        }
    }
}
